## 2026-04-15 (Suppress relation-candidate panel when no pending review)
- What changed:
  - Adjusted [LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx](/d:/06-project/expo_duo/duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx) rendering logic:
    - `Relation Candidate Review` section now requires actual pending candidates (`pendingReview > 0` or non-empty candidate list).
    - Removed default auto-display of this diagnostics-heavy panel when batch has no pending review items.
- What was learned:
  - Persisting `batchId` is useful for continuity, but showing full candidate diagnostics by default increases cognitive noise when there is nothing to review.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm run lint -- components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx` passed.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional future UX: keep an explicit "Show batch diagnostics" toggle for expert users.

## 2026-04-15 (Import panel UI hierarchy cleanup for template actions)
- What changed:
  - Refined [LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx](/d:/06-project/expo_duo/duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx) interaction hierarchy:
    - removed template download buttons from the primary action row,
    - moved them into a secondary utility area labeled `Templates (Optional)`,
    - applied lighter styling so templates no longer compete with core import actions.
- What was learned:
  - Keeping optional tools at the same visual level as primary workflow actions increases operator scanning cost and creates action ambiguity.
  - Demoting optional actions to a clear secondary tier aligns with one-screen/one-goal cognitive-load policy.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm run lint -- components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx src/storage/lexicalAssetImportSessionStorage.ts` passed.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If optional tools continue to be noisy, move them under an explicit expandable "More tools" toggle.

## 2026-04-15 (Import panel stale parse warning cleanup + batch restore)
- What changed:
  - Updated import session storage key to `@duoxx:lexical_asset_import_session_v2` in [lexicalAssetImportSessionStorage.ts](/d:/06-project/expo_duo/duoxx/src/storage/lexicalAssetImportSessionStorage.ts).
  - Added persisted `batchId` to import session model.
  - Updated [LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx](/d:/06-project/expo_duo/duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx):
    - hydrate `batchId` and auto-run `refreshBatchState(batchId)` after page refresh,
    - on successful `createImportBatch`, clear `review/fileName/fileType/bundleReviews` to prevent old parser warnings from staying on screen,
    - persist `review: null` when batch is already created.
- What was learned:
  - The repeated "Re-upload" button and persistent warning list came from intentional session persistence of `review` plus `fileName`.
  - For operator flow, once batch is created, keeping parser issues visible is confusing; batch review should become the primary context.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm run lint -- components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx src/storage/lexicalAssetImportSessionStorage.ts` passed.

## 2026-04-15 (Lexical import parser routing fix for plural structured headers)
- What changed:
  - Updated [lexicalSingleFileImport.ts](/d:/06-project/expo_duo/duoxx/src/services/lexicalSingleFileImport.ts:1178) markdown structured-asset detector.
  - Added plural header recognition for structured assets:
    - `collocations`, `phrases`, `sentencePatterns`, `idioms`, `spokenExpressions` (and singular variants).
  - This prevents structured markdown files from being misrouted to word-parser mode, which caused large `ORPHAN_FIELD` warning counts.
- What was learned:
  - The upload issue was parser mode selection mismatch, not missing data in source markdown.
  - When structured header is not matched, every `## ...` line is treated as plain key-value outside word block and floods warnings.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm test -- src/services/__tests__/assetParseDiagnostics.test.ts --runInBand` passed.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add an optional auto-run import path in Review Hub import tab (upload -> create batch -> refresh report), while still stopping before publish for manual review.

## 2026-04-14 (Knowledge absorb breadcrumb rule clarified as explicit 2+ depth)
- What changed:
  - Refined `duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` breadcrumb visibility logic with explicit boolean:
    - `const shouldShowBreadcrumb = navigationStack.length >= 2`.
  - Rewired breadcrumb row rendering and title offset to use `shouldShowBreadcrumb`.
  - This locks the expected behavior:
    - depth `1`: hide root breadcrumb chip,
    - depth `2+`: show full breadcrumb levels (including first and current).
- What was learned:
  - Making depth rule explicit avoids interpretation drift from scattered inline length checks.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm run lint -- app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` passed.

## 2026-04-14 (Knowledge absorb: hide breadcrumb when only one node)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` breadcrumb rendering condition from `navigationStack.length > 0` to `navigationStack.length > 1`.
  - Updated title spacing condition to match breadcrumb visibility rule (`cardTitleWithBreadcrumb` now applies only when breadcrumb is actually shown).
  - Result: when there is only one current node (no real path), the first breadcrumb chip is hidden.
- What was learned:
  - Single-node state is a “current card” state, not a breadcrumb state; showing a one-item breadcrumb increases visual noise and duplicates the title.
- Verification:
  - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
  - `duoxx`: `npm run lint -- app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` passed.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If needed, apply the same “min 2 nodes” rule to any other page that reuses breadcrumb UI patterns.

    - push breadcrumb stack,

## 2026-04-10 (Graph search: active scope keyword fallback to published snapshot)
- What changed:
  - Updated backend node search in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/lexiconGraphService.js`:
    - In `listNodes(scope='active')`, when keyword search returns 0 active hits, the service now automatically retries against the active published snapshot and returns matched rows.
    - Added response meta flags for transparency: `fallbackScope: 'published'`, `fallbackReason: 'active_keyword_miss'`, `snapshotVersion`.
  - Added integration coverage in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/__tests__/lexiconGraphService.integration.test.js`:
    - Verifies normal active hit (`run`) stays on active results.
    - Verifies fallback hit (`go`) is returned from snapshot when active has no match.
  - Updated frontend types in `duoxx/src/services/lexiconApi.ts` to include fallback meta fields.
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/LexiconGraphExplorerPanel.tsx` to display a hint when active-search results are coming from published snapshot fallback.
  - Verification:
    - `duoxx`: `npx tsc --noEmit` passed.
    - backend JS syntax: `node --check src/services/lexiconGraphService.js` passed.
- What was learned:
  - The admin “active nodes” source and learner-facing snapshot source can diverge; pure active-scope search can miss terms users see in learning cards.
  - A scoped fallback keeps operator search usable without changing existing scope controls.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - In a backend environment with dependencies installed, run `jest src/services/__tests__/lexiconGraphService.integration.test.js` to validate runtime behavior.
  - Decide whether to keep fallback as long-term behavior or add an explicit “search both scopes” toggle later.

## 2026-04-03 (Investigate/fix browser automation channel Transport closed)
- What changed:
  - Reproduced failure on both browser toolchains: `mcp__playwright__*` and `mcp__chrome_devtools__*` both returned `Transport closed`.
  - Verified local binaries were healthy (`chrome-devtools-mcp --help`, `npx @playwright/mcp@latest --help` both worked), narrowing issue to session transport layer.
  - Cleared VSCode extension Codex app-server processes (`openai.chatgpt` codex.exe) to remove possible competing Codex runtime.
  - Recycled Codex desktop `app-server` process and re-checked tool health.
  - Confirmed recovery: browser MCP calls now succeed (`browser_tabs` and `list_pages` return normal payload).
- What was learned:
  - Simultaneous `Transport closed` on both browser stacks is a connection-layer symptom, not page/test logic.
  - In this environment, a minimal Codex app-server recycle can restore MCP channels without restarting the full desktop app.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If issue repeats, prioritize capturing exact timestamp + app-server PID transitions to improve confidence on root-cause attribution.

## 2026-03-20 (Mongo lexical quiz option migration + distractor hardening)
- What changed:
  - Added backend helper `\\wsl.localhost\Ubuntu-22.04\home\rookie\project\duoxx_server\src\services\lexicalQuizOptionRules.js` and test `...\lexicalQuizOptionRules.test.js` to normalize translation-choice options with deterministic rotation and Chinese-translation-only distractors.
  - Added backend migration script `\\wsl.localhost\Ubuntu-22.04\home\rookie\project\duoxx_server\scripts\migrate-lexical-quiz-options-v1.js` plus package script `migrate:lexical-quiz-options-v1` for dry-run/apply rewriting of legacy `translation_choice / word_card` options in `SeedQuiz` and `GeneratedQuizVersion`.
  - Kept Turing's distractor-quality upgrade in place for current generation/local fallback: same POS first, then closer difficulty, then overlapping scene tags; `true/false` and non-Chinese answers are excluded.
  - Removed the accidental local fake `D:\06-project\expo_duo\duoxx_server` directory after copying the real helper/test into the actual backend workspace.
- What was learned:
  - The real backend lives under the WSL workspace; writing to a same-named local Windows folder silently creates dead files that the server never uses.
  - Old lexical quiz rows can now be normalized safely in dry-run mode before any write, which is the right guardrail for production Mongo cleanup.
  - Current lexical asset data does not reliably carry difficulty/scene metadata yet, so the new distractor scoring must treat those fields as optional and degrade gracefully back to POS-first matching.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Run the migration with `--apply` in the actual target environment after reviewing the dry-run output.
  - Decide whether to extract the shared distractor rules into one cross-runtime source or keep the server/helper and frontend fallback implementations separate.

## 2026-03-23 (Exercise Review duplicate judgment-question dedupe)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx_server/src/services/lexicalQuizService.js` so review-list loading deduplicates identical quizzes by semantic signature before the operator UI sees them.
  - Added generation-side duplicate suppression so `translation_choice` / `true_false` generation skips writing a new row when the visible question would match an existing seed or generated quiz.
  - Added backend regression coverage in `duoxx_server/src/services/__tests__/lexicalQuizService.test.js` for both review dedupe and duplicate-skip generation.
- What was learned:
  - The duplicate judgment questions were not a renderer problem; the service layer was returning both seed and generated rows for the same visible question.
  - Preventing duplicates at generation time is necessary, but review-list dedupe is still useful for historical Mongo data that already contains duplicates.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Smoke-test one legacy course in the learner after the backend change.
  - If historical Mongo duplication keeps surfacing in old courses, add a one-time cleanup migration keyed by the same semantic signature.

## 2026-03-04
- What changed:
  - Upgraded `duoxx_server` pipeline extraction to support scanned PDF documents via OCR fallback:
    - Added `src/pipeline/utils/pdfOcr.ts` using `pdf-to-png-converter` + `tesseract.js` + local `eng/chi_sim` language data.
    - Updated `src/pipeline/agents/ingestAgent.ts` to auto-switch from `pdf-parse` to OCR when direct text extraction is empty/weak.
    - Default OCR coverage now processes up to 30 pages (`PIPELINE_OCR_MAX_PAGES` override supported).
  - Added vocabulary-focused structuring for English word-list documents:
    - `src/pipeline/agents/structureAgent.ts` now detects vocabulary lines and generates `vocabulary_card` exercises with metadata (word/phonetic/translation/example/sourceSection).
    - `src/pipeline/types.ts` extended with `vocabulary_card` type and exercise metadata fields.
    - `src/pipeline/agents/domainEnglishAgent.ts` now validates vocabulary-card required fields.
  - Upgraded admin UI to inspect/edit vocabulary cards:
    - `src/public/pipeline-admin.html` added `vocabulary_card` type and dedicated vocab editor panel.
    - `src/public/pipeline-admin.js` renders vocab details in list and supports editing word/phonetic/translation/example fields.
  - Added OCR/runtime dependencies in `duoxx_server/package.json` and refreshed lockfile.
- What was learned:
  - The uploaded `15????????500??pdf` is scan-image based; `pdf-parse` alone returns mostly empty text.
  - OCR fallback is necessary for Chinese/English mixed vocabulary sheets; full-run extraction produced ~1526 vocabulary cards from the sample file.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Consider adding async job progress updates for long OCR runs (~2+ minutes on multi-page files).
  - Improve vocabulary parser accuracy for broken OCR lines and multi-column edge cases.

## 2026-03-04 (runtime stability fix)
- What changed:
  - Fixed backend startup crash caused by OCR native optional dependency loading too early.
  - Refactored `src/pipeline/utils/pdfOcr.ts` to lazy-load `pdf-to-png-converter` and `tesseract.js` only when OCR fallback is actually used.
  - Updated `src/pipeline/agents/ingestAgent.ts` to treat OCR as best-effort fallback and avoid crashing extraction flow when OCR runtime is temporarily unavailable.
  - Updated orchestrator load error text in `src/services/contentPipelineService.js` to include both `npm i` and `npm run build:pipeline`.
  - Re-ran dependency install in WSL and rebuilt pipeline to regenerate `dist-pipeline`.
- What was learned:
  - Importing OCR stack at module top-level can crash service boot when optional native bindings are missing/corrupted, even before any job runs.
  - Lazy loading + graceful fallback keeps API startup stable while still supporting OCR when environment is healthy.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add explicit health check endpoint for OCR runtime (`available/unavailable` + reason) so UI can warn before users start long jobs.

## 2026-03-04 (structured data direct-to-course flow)
- What changed:
  - Added structured source mode support across backend pipeline:
    - `src/pipeline/types.ts`: added `SourceInputMode` and CSV format support.
    - `src/pipeline/agents/ingestAgent.ts`: supports `.csv` and stores `inputMode`.
    - `src/models/ContentPipelineJob.js`: added `source.mode` (`auto` / `structured`) and CSV format enum.
    - `src/services/contentPipelineService.js`: accepts `sourceMode`, persists it, and passes mode into orchestrator run input.
    - `src/routes/pipeline.js`: accepts `sourceMode` in `POST /jobs`.
  - Implemented domain-focused structured curriculum generation:
    - Added `src/pipeline/agents/structuredDataTeacherAgent.ts`.
    - Agent parses structured `.csv`, markdown tables in `.md`, and delimited/list-style `.txt`.
    - Generates review-ready draft courses with:
      - vocabulary cards (`vocabulary_card`)
      - teacher-designed translation questions
      - teacher-designed multiple-choice questions
    - Integrated this agent into `src/pipeline/agents/structureAgent.ts` before generic fallback extraction.
  - Updated admin page UX (`src/public/pipeline-admin.html`, `src/public/pipeline-admin.js`):
    - new button: `??????????? (for `.csv/.md/.txt`)
    - mode badge: `???: ?????? / ????????
    - selected mode is sent to backend on job creation.
- What was learned:
  - A dedicated structured mode significantly improves predictable conversion from tabular/list data to reviewable courses.
  - Keeping the generated draft in the existing review UI enables immediate human QA without extra pages.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add progress indicator per stage for long structured imports with large row counts.
  - Optionally add downloadable parse report (rows accepted/rejected + reasons) to help operators fix source files quickly.

## 2026-03-06 (pipeline redesign technical specification)
- What changed:
  - Added technical spec for V1 pipeline redesign:
    - `duoxx_server/docs/pipeline-redesign/SPEC-v1-course-production-web.md`
  - Defined Agent Team architecture and lifecycle:
    - runtime: create per "start processing" request
    - skills: configuration-time reusable rule assets
  - Defined V1 interface strategy:
    - keep existing `/jobs` internals
    - add simplified facade API (`/process`, paginated courses, write-db upsert)
  - Defined page state machine, permission matrix, vocabulary-card CRUD model, and error code contract.
- What was learned:
  - User expects deterministic and simple runtime behavior: agents are runtime workers, skills are static capability packs.
  - Frontend must consume a simplified process API to hide orchestration complexity.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Split implementation into milestones and test plans before coding.

  - A milestone-first approach is required to avoid rework from UI-first implementation.

## 2026-03-06 (M5 hardening: facade payload validation)
- What changed:
  - Added strict payload/query validator module:
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/pipelineDraftValidator.js`
    - validates:
      - `POST /api/pipeline/process` input (`sourcePath`, `displayName`)
      - `GET /api/pipeline/courses` query (`page`, `limit`, `language`, `keyword`)
      - `POST /api/pipeline/courses/write` payload and full draft structure
  - Added vocabulary-card field-level constraints before write-db:
    - `metadata.word`, `metadata.translation` required
    - `synonyms` / `antonyms` must be string arrays
    - length limits for phonetic/pos/example fields
    - answer/options type checks for non-vocabulary exercises
  - Added vocabulary draft integrity rule:
    - if all exercises are `vocabulary_card`, draft must contain exactly one lesson
  - Integrated validators into route facade:
    - updated `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`
    - standardized 400 responses with `code`, `error`, `details` for validation failures
- What was learned:
  - Frontend simplicity needs backend guardrails; otherwise malformed draft payload can silently enter write-db flow.
  - Keeping first error in `error` while returning full `details` balances UI compatibility and debugging depth.
- Validation:
  - `node --check src/services/pipelineDraftValidator.js`
  - `node --check src/routes/pipeline.js`
  - `npm run build:pipeline`
  - `npm test -- --runInBand` => 3 suites, 11 tests passed
  - Added tests:
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/pipelineDraftValidator.test.js`
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add role model (`admin` / `operator`) to `User` and apply route-level role guard for pipeline write actions.
  - Remove or isolate legacy `/jobs`/review/publish routes if no longer needed in V1 production UI.

## 2026-03-06 (M5 hardening: role-based access control)
- What changed:
  - Added role model support to user schema:
    - `duoxx_server/src/models/User.js`
    - new field: `role` (`admin` | `operator`), default `operator`
  - Added reusable role middleware in auth layer:
    - `duoxx_server/src/middleware/auth.js`
    - `resolveUserRole(user)` with backward-compatible fallback to `operator`
    - `authorizeRoles(...roles)` middleware with 401/403 handling
  - Applied role guards to pipeline routes:
    - `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`
    - all pipeline routes now require `admin` or `operator`
    - legacy review/publish endpoints restricted to `admin` only:
      - `PATCH /jobs/:jobId/review-checklist`
      - `POST /jobs/:jobId/review`
      - `POST /jobs/:jobId/publish`
      - `GET /review/tasks`
  - Added middleware tests:
    - `duoxx_server/src/middleware/auth.test.js`
    - covers: missing-user 401, operator/admin allow logic, legacy no-role compatibility, admin-only deny, invalid config throw
- What was learned:
  - A fallback role strategy is necessary to avoid breaking legacy users that were created before `role` field existed.
  - Restricting legacy review/publish endpoints to admin isolates old flow while keeping V1 operator production path intact.
- Validation:
  - `node --check src/middleware/auth.js`
  - `node --check src/routes/pipeline.js`
  - `node --check src/models/User.js`
  - `npm run build:pipeline`
  - `npm test -- --runInBand` => 4 suites, 17 tests passed
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add admin UI/API for role assignment (promote/demote operator) instead of relying on direct DB edits.
  - Decide whether to fully retire legacy `/jobs` review/publish API group in next milestone.

## 2026-03-06 (Codex MCP setup: chrome-devtools)
- What changed:
  - Installed global npm package `chrome-devtools-mcp` (version `0.19.0`) on the local Windows environment.

    - added `[mcp_servers.chrome_devtools]`
    - set `command = "chrome-devtools-mcp"`
- What was learned:
  - `chrome-devtools-mcp` is the official npm package name; scoped package `@chrome-devtools/mcp` is not available on npm.
  - Existing Codex session does not hot-load new MCP servers; a new session/restart is required to see `chrome_devtools`.
- Validation:
  - `chrome-devtools-mcp --version` => `0.19.0`
  - `chrome-devtools-mcp --help` executed successfully.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Restart Codex session to load the new `chrome_devtools` MCP server into tool registry.

    - covers query/pagination normalization, invalid role rejection, self-update rejection, not-found handling, and success path
  - Extended auth routes with admin-only role management endpoints:
    - `GET /api/auth/users?keyword=&page=&limit=`
    - `PATCH /api/auth/users/:userId/role` body: `{ role: 'admin'|'operator' }`
    - file: `duoxx_server/src/routes/auth.js`
  - Reused existing RBAC middleware (`authenticate + authorizeRoles('admin')`) for new endpoints.
- What was learned:
  - Separating role management into a service keeps auth routes thin and makes permission-sensitive logic easier to unit-test.
  - Blocking self role change avoids accidental admin lockout during manual operations.
- Validation:
  - `node --check src/services/userRoleService.js`
  - `node --check src/routes/auth.js`
  - `node --check src/models/User.js`
  - `npm run build:pipeline`
  - `npm test -- --runInBand` => 5 suites, 23 tests passed
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add a lightweight admin web page section to call `/api/auth/users` and `/api/auth/users/:id/role` directly.
  - Consider adding audit log records for role changes (who changed whom, old/new role, timestamp).

## 2026-03-09 (/admin/pipeline TTS + explanation review V1)
- What changed:
  - Frontend (`d:\06-project\expo_duo\duoxx`):
    - Reworked `components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` to support content-level operations on sentence/word/phrase.
    - Added sentence-level TTS actions: generate/regenerate and play from saved asset URL.
    - Added explanation review workflow UI: open target -> prompt hint -> generate draft -> structured field editing -> approve/reject.
    - Added pending-review sidebar (`pending_review`) with quick open by locator.
    - Added structured payload editors for `zhSummary`, `enSummary`, `breakdown[]`, `pitfalls[]`, `memoryTips[]`.
  - Frontend API layer:
    - Extended `src/services/pipelineApi.ts` with `ContentLocator`, explanation schema types, and calls for generate/list/patch/approve/reject + TTS generate.
    - Extended `src/services/apiClient.ts` with `PATCH` request support and fixed malformed timeout/network fallback messages.
  - Backend (`duoxx_server`):
    - Added `src/services/contentLocator.js` + tests (`contentLocator.test.js`) for normalized locator protocol and source resolution.
    - Added `src/models/CourseExplanationDraft.js` and model export in `src/models/index.js`.
    - Extended `src/services/contentPipelineService.js` with:
      - TTS generation + file persistence (`uploads/pipeline-tts`) + payload upsert by locator.
      - Explanation draft generation, edit, approve, reject, list workflow.
      - Structured payload normalization/validation and approved asset upsert into `exercise.reviewAssets.explanations`.
    - Extended `src/routes/pipeline.js` with endpoints:
      - `POST /courses/:courseId/tts/generate`
      - `POST /courses/:courseId/explanations/generate`
      - `GET /courses/:courseId/explanations`
      - `PATCH /explanations/:draftId`
      - `POST /explanations/:draftId/approve`
      - `POST /explanations/:draftId/reject`
    - Added static serving for `/uploads` in `src/app.js` and fixed malformed legacy strings that broke JS parsing.
    - Replaced/expanded `src/services/contentPipelineService.test.js` to cover TTS locator upsert and explanation lifecycle.
- What was learned:
  - Locator-key upsert is sufficient for V1 idempotency: repeated TTS/explanation approvals replace prior asset at same content location.
  - Draft workflow can stay isolated in `CourseExplanationDraft` while approved assets are embedded directly in `PublishedCourse.payload.exercise.reviewAssets`.
  - Existing repo has unrelated TypeScript errors; file-level transpile/lint checks are required to verify changed frontend files without blocking on historical issues.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add backend route/integration tests for HTTP-level behavior (status codes + payload writes).
  - Add frontend automated interaction tests for TTS and explanation approval panel.
  - Consider showing locator jump/highlight in middle panel when clicking pending draft for faster reviewer navigation.

  - Rewrote backend startup/log text to ASCII English in:
    - `duoxx_server/src/app.js`
    - `duoxx_server/src/config/env.js`
  - Kept behavior unchanged while removing garbled/mojibake runtime output.
- What was learned:
  - In this environment, browser access to WSL service is not reliably forwarded via localhost; explicit portproxy is required.
  - Mojibake came from source-string encoding mismatch, not from business logic.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If WSL IP changes after restart, refresh portproxy rule to the new IP.
  - Optionally automate portproxy refresh via startup script.

    - updateExplanationDraft now sends draftId + structuredPayload + promptHint.
    - approveExplanationDraft now sends only draftId.
    - rejectExplanationDraft now sends fixed reason Rejected by reviewer without note.
- What was learned:
  - Operators only need prompt editing and approve/reject actions here; extra note field adds noise.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If reviewers still need annotations later, consider storing internal operator logs separately from the approve/reject form.

## 2026-03-10 (pipeline duplicate-course root-cause check)
- What changed:
  - Investigated why `/admin/pipeline` shows duplicate course title `15閿熷眾鑳岄敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷烽敓?500閿熸枻鎷穈.
  - Confirmed duplicates are real DB records in `publishedcourses`, not frontend rendering duplication.
  - Verified two active records exist for same `title + language` with different `_id`, `version`, and `sourceJobId`.
  - Traced backend logic:
    - `src/services/contentPipelineService.js` `writeCourse` create branch always inserts a new `PublishedCourse` when `courseId` is absent.
    - `src/services/contentPipelineService.js` `listCourses` returns all active records directly (no dedupe/latest-only grouping).
    - `src/models/PublishedCourse.js` has no uniqueness constraint for active natural key (`title/language` or source job mapping).
- What was learned:
  - Duplicate title entries happen when the same course is published multiple times via different source jobs without reusing `courseId`.
  - Current schema/version strategy supports multiple versions, but list API is not collapsing versions for admin display.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Decide desired rule: keep one active row per logical course (archive older), or keep multi-version but list latest only.
  - Then enforce at service+DB level (upsert/unique index or status-aware partial unique index).

  - Fixed mojibake/garbled Chinese UI labels in `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx`.
  - Replaced corrupted strings in course mode selector, table headers (`閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹/閿熸枻鎷烽敓绲?, action button states (`閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹/閿熸磥杈?閿熺潾闈╂嫹`), and exercise-edit modal labels/placeholders/buttons.

  - The reported 閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷?item 閿熸枻鎷烽敓璇€?came from corrupted frontend literals in the admin page, not from latest DB course payload encoding.

## 2026-03-10 (L5閿熸枻鎷疯嫬閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹婧愰敓鏂ゆ嫹寮忛敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷?
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/src/components/exercises/MultipleChoiceExercise.tsx` to stop forcing line breaks after numeric prefix + em-dash in question stems.
  - New behavior keeps stems in one line (unless source already contains explicit newline), and normalizes legacy pattern like `4. 閿熸枻鎷稨ello` to `4. Hello`.
- What was learned:
  - The visible `4.` / `Hello` split is caused by frontend formatting logic, not user action.
  - Additional content integrity risk exists in source CSV: unquoted commas in exercise stem rows can split fields and truncate stems during import.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Introduce strict source schema and pre-import lint gate for exercise rows to reject malformed CSV before build/import.
  - Optionally migrate authoring format to JSONL/Markdown+YAML canonical assets, with CSV generated as review/export view only.

    - `duoxx/resources/7U/review/question-assets.ndjson`

    - `course:assets:lint:7u`
    - `course:assets:export:7u`
- What was learned:
  - Current line-break symptom had two layers: frontend normalization bug and upstream CSV row-quality risk.
  - A stable NDJSON source-of-truth with review status metadata is safer than direct authoring in mixed CSV when English commas are frequent.

  - Relaxed `validateCourseWritePayload` to allow write requests without `sourceJobId` when they can resolve to update path by natural key.

  - Updated one source job reference from deleted course id to kept course id.
- What was learned:
  - Duplicate active courses were caused by create-on-write behavior when `courseId` was omitted.
  - Even after data cleanup, list-side dedupe is still needed as a guardrail.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional hard constraint: add DB-level unique policy for active natural key (title+language+status) after evaluating migration risk.

  - Executed backfill successfully for current DB.

  - Existing course docs had no sequential business id; Mongo `_id` uniqueness alone did not satisfy operator serial-number requirement.

## 2026-03-11 (vocab course 3500 lesson sanitization + reusable cleaned asset)
- What changed:
  - Added runtime sanitizer `duoxx/src/services/learningLessonSanitizer.ts` for remote lesson payloads.
  - Added course-specific asset patch table `duoxx/src/data/vocabCourseAssetPatches.ts` (drop 13 known dirty rows for `vocab-course-69aaafeac973401a4d7270e7`).
  - Updated `duoxx/app/lesson-exercise/[lessonId].tsx` to sanitize remote vocab lessons and fallback to local cleaned asset when needed.
  - Enhanced `duoxx/src/components/exercises/FillBlankExercise.tsx`: if sentence has no `___`, render standalone answer input.
  - Added reusable cleaned asset export script `duoxx/scripts/course-import/export-vocab-lesson-clean.js` and npm script `course:assets:export:vocab-clean`.
  - Generated reusable asset file `duoxx/resources/vocab/15day3500.cleaned.lesson.json` (+ README).
  - Added tests `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/learningLessonSanitizer.test.ts`.
- What was learned:
  - Root cause is mixed data quality in remote vocab lesson payloads: all fill-blank prompts lacked `___`, and some category-summary rows were imported as exercises.
  - A sanitizer+patch model provides immediate runtime stability while preserving a path to upstream data source repair.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Move the same cleaning rules to backend course export/import so mobile/web no longer needs runtime patching.
  - Add a strict lint gate for vocab assets before publishing to avoid summary/meta rows entering exercise collections.

## 2026-03-11 (frontend backend-fallback ban enforced in lesson flow)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/app/lesson-exercise/[lessonId].tsx` to remove runtime backend-data fallback behavior for vocab routes:
    - removed sanitizer/static JSON fallback path
    - added strict backend contract validation (`exerciseModuleIds` alignment, fill_blank placeholder, answers non-empty)
    - backend payload invalid/missing now enters explicit error state instead of silent fallback
    - header/completion title now uses course display title with priority `source.title` -> `lesson.title`
  - Updated `duoxx/src/components/exercises/FillBlankExercise.tsx` to remove no-placeholder input fallback; now shows contract error and disables submit when `___` missing.
  - Updated `duoxx/DATA_QUALITY_CONSTITUTION.md` to ban frontend data-healing fallback, with only presentation-only mapping (e.g., i18n labels) as allowed exception.
- What was learned:
  - Silent frontend fallback hides backend contract drift and causes title/data inconsistency across list/detail pages.
  - Contract-first rendering (fail-fast + telemetry/error state) makes backend ownership boundaries enforceable.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Remove/retire remaining sanitizer patch artifacts (`learningLessonSanitizer`, static cleaned lesson fallback asset references) once backend import pipeline is fully fixed.
  - Add CI grep/lint rule to block future reintroduction of runtime lesson fallback patterns.

## 2026-03-11 (pipeline JSX unicode text-node rendering fix)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` to replace JSX text-node unicode escape literals with real display text.
  - Fixed table headers and row action text that rendered as raw `\\uXXXX` in UI:
    - `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`, `閿熸枻鎷烽敓绲? row action `閿熸磥杈慲, selection mark `?`.
  - Verified with targeted lint: `npm run lint -- --no-error-on-unmatched-pattern components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` (pass).
- What was learned:
  - In JSX text nodes, `\\uXXXX` is rendered literally; unicode escape decoding only happens inside JS string literals/expressions.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: run a repo grep for `>\\u[0-9a-fA-F]{4}` on admin components to prevent similar regressions.

## 2026-03-12 (settings child-account delete flow cross-platform fix)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/app/settings.tsx` child-account delete flow to split into confirm + execute steps:
    - `confirmDeleteChildAccount(account)`
    - `executeDeleteChildAccount(account)`
  - Added cross-platform confirmation behavior:
    - Web uses `globalThis.confirm(...)`
    - Native keeps `Alert.alert(...)` with Promise-based resolve.
  - Replaced delete-result alert-only feedback with inline feedback (`childFormError` / `childFormSuccess`) so users always see outcome.
  - Added row-scoped delete loading key (`delete:<childId>`) and in-row `鍒犻敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷?..` state, avoiding prior global lock behavior from `Boolean(childActionLoadingId)`.
  - Kept UI structure minimal (same delete entry icon), no extra modal/card layer.
  - Added automated coverage in `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/familyAccountService.test.ts`:
    - `deletes child account and shrinks child list`.
- What was learned:
  - `Alert.alert` button callback flow is unreliable for RN Web confirmation UX; explicit Web confirm branch avoids no-op deletion behavior.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: extract confirm helper into shared utility for consistent cross-platform destructive actions across pages.
## 2026-03-12 (settings child-account inline success messages removed)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/app/settings.tsx` to remove all inline success messages in child-account area.
  - Removed `childFormSuccess` state, all `setChildFormSuccess(...)` writes, success `<Text>` rendering block, and `childFormSuccessText` style.
  - Kept inline error feedback (`childFormError`) unchanged.
  - Kept create/reset/delete behavior and delete confirm/loading logic unchanged.
  - Verified via `npm run lint -- --no-error-on-unmatched-pattern app/settings.tsx`.
- What was learned:
  - For this screen, users prefer low-noise operation feedback and only want actionable error visibility.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: if needed later, replace removed success text with subtle non-persistent toast to avoid layout shifts.
## 2026-03-12 (swipe entry merged into learning tab; standalone tab removed)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/app/(tabs)/_layout.tsx` to remove the standalone `swipe-learning` bottom tab; tabs now keep `瀛︿範 / 閿熻娇绛规嫹 / 閿熸彮纰夋嫹` only.
  - Updated `duoxx/app/(tabs)/index.tsx` to add a high-priority `鍒烽敓鏂ゆ嫹瀛﹁嫳閿熸枻鎷穈 card at the top of the learning page tool section, routing to `/modules/swipe-learning`.

  - Updated `duoxx/src/modules/swipe-learning/screens/SwipeLearningScreen.tsx` to fully own the swipe screen implementation in module layer and removed reverse dependency on app route files.
- What was learned:
  - Keeping `app route -> src module` one-way ownership avoids route-level coupling and makes future navigation refactors lower-risk.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add a small route-level smoke test to assert `/modules/swipe-learning` remains reachable after future tab/layout changes.
## 2026-03-12 (sentence-rule decoupling v1 cutover)
- What changed:
  - Backend learning contract switched to snapshot protocol:
    - Reworked `duoxx_server/src/routes/learning.js` to serve lesson data from `LessonItemRef + ExerciseSnapshot + SentenceAsset`.
    - `/api/learning/lesson-exercise/:lessonId` now returns fill_blank using `sentence + tokens + gaps` (no `___` dependency).
    - `/api/learning/courses` now dedupes by `title+language` and keeps latest version.
  - Added backend migration/import tooling:
    - `duoxx_server/scripts/migrate-sentence-rule-v1.js` (one-time migration from `PublishedCourse.payload` to sentence/rule/snapshot/ref chain).
    - `duoxx_server/scripts/lint-sentence-rule-csv.js` (hard lint gate for `sentences.csv`, `rules.csv`, `lesson_bindings.csv`).
    - `duoxx_server/scripts/import-sentence-rule-csv.js` (CSV import + precompile snapshot upsert).
    - `duoxx_server/scripts/lib/sentenceRuleCsv.js` (CSV parsing/normalization helpers).
    - Added npm scripts in `duoxx_server/package.json` for migrate/lint/import.
  - Added backend tests:
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/sentenceRuleCompiler.test.js`
    - `duoxx_server/src/routes/learning.test.js`
  - Frontend fill_blank protocol migrated:
    - Extended `duoxx/src/models/exercise.ts` with `FillBlankToken` and `FillBlankGap`.
    - Reworked `duoxx/src/components/exercises/FillBlankExercise.tsx` to render by token-gap protocol (legacy marker fallback retained only for old data safety).
    - Updated `duoxx/src/validators/fillBlankValidator.ts` and test for multi-gap validation.
    - Updated `duoxx/src/services/lessonEngine.ts` to accept `string | string[]` fill_blank answers.
    - Rewrote `duoxx/app/lesson-exercise/[lessonId].tsx` contract validation to require `tokens+gaps` for fill_blank modules.
- What was learned:
  - Frontend `___` placeholder contract is the direct source of runtime drift; token-gap protocol is stable and replay-friendly.
  - Running backend test commands from Windows UNC path breaks `cross-env`; invoke through WSL shell (`wsl ... bash -lc`).
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Run `migrate:sentence-rule-v1 --apply` on target DB and verify key lesson IDs now resolve through snapshot refs.
  - Publish authoritative CSV templates/examples for `sentences.csv/rules.csv/lesson_bindings.csv` to upstream content producers.
  - Remove remaining legacy marker assumptions from non-core modules once old payloads are fully migrated.
## 2026-03-12 (/admin/pipeline rule-template enhancement v2 baseline)
- What changed:
  - Backend V2 rule/candidate domain added:
    - `duoxx_server/src/models/ExerciseCandidate.js` (candidate review queue).
    - `duoxx_server/src/models/SentenceAssetChange.js` (sentence asset change review).
    - Extended `duoxx_server/src/models/RuleTemplate.js` with `targetSelector`, `outputSpec`, `operatorIds`, `difficultyPolicy`, `enabled`.
    - Updated `duoxx_server/src/models/index.js` exports.
  - Backend engine + service flow implemented:
    - Added `duoxx_server/src/services/ruleTemplateEngine.js` (rule matching + candidate generation, supports one-sentence multi-rule matches and multi-outputSpec outputs).
    - Extended `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js` with:
      - sentence asset list/create/change-review methods,
      - rule template CRUD/version/state methods,
      - preview generation (`preview` non-persistent),
      - candidate generation/list/update/approve/reject,
      - approval writes `ExerciseSnapshot + LessonItemRef`.

    - `GET/POST /sentence-assets`,
    - `PATCH /sentence-assets/:sentenceId/changes`,
    - `GET /sentence-asset-changes`, `POST .../:changeId/approve|reject`,
    - `GET/POST /rule-templates`,
    - `POST /rule-templates/:ruleId/version`,
    - `PATCH /rule-templates/:ruleId/:ruleVersion`,
    - `POST /rule-templates/:ruleId/preview`,

    - `GET/PATCH/POST /exercise-candidates*` review endpoints.

    - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` to expose `Rules V2` entry and open the new workbench modal.
- What was learned:
  - Existing `PipelineDashboard.tsx` had multiple historical mojibake fragments that can silently break JSX parsing; linting this file after edits is mandatory.
  - One-to-many matching should stay server-side so preview and candidate review remain deterministic and traceable per `ruleId/ruleVersion`.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add dedicated integration tests for new pipeline endpoints (`preview`, `generate-candidates`, `approve/reject`).
  - Extend review UI with bulk approve/reject and inline draftPayload editor safety checks (JSON schema validation).
  - Add formal migration/backfill script for existing rule templates to populate new V2 fields consistently.
## 2026-03-12 (/admin/pipeline v2 follow-up: batch candidate review + evidence view)
- What changed:
  - Backend:
    - Added batch review endpoint `POST /api/pipeline/exercise-candidates/bulk-review` in `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`.
    - Added service method `bulkReviewExerciseCandidates()` in `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`, supporting batch approve/reject with per-item failure isolation.
  - Frontend API:
    - Extended `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts` with `bulkReviewExerciseCandidates()` and `BulkReviewExerciseCandidatesResult`.
  - Frontend admin UI:
    - Upgraded `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` candidate tab with:
      - multi-select checkboxes,
      - `Select All` toggle,
      - `Batch Approve` / `Batch Reject` actions,
      - explicit column layout (`Rule`, `KnowledgePoint`, `Sentence`, `Status`, `Actions`).
    - Upgraded preview tab to display match evidence summary (`reason`, token indices, condition summary).
- What was learned:
  - Batch review should continue-on-error and return partial failures instead of aborting whole operation.
  - For reviewer efficiency, evidence summary and source-rule columns are more important than dense card details.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add candidate JSON inline edit modal with schema guard (to prevent malformed payload writes).
  - Add backend integration tests for `bulk-review` (approve + reject + mixed-failure cases).

## 2026-03-12 (Rules V2 Studio simplification: sentence+rule direct apply)
- What changed:
  - Reworked `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` to add a default `Studio` tab.
  - `Studio` now shows:
    - sentence list (search + single select),
    - rule list (search + multi-select + select-all),
    - generated exercise series panel (preview candidates + generated candidate rows).
  - Added direct actions for operators:
    - `Preview Selected` (runs selected rules against selected sentence),
    - `Generate Series` (creates candidates for selected sentence + selected rules).
  - Kept existing advanced tabs (`Rules/Preview/Candidates/Sentences`) for power workflows.
- What was learned:
  - Operators need one-screen "select sentence + select rules + see output" flow; rule-json forms are still useful but should be secondary.
  - Running per-selected-rule requests keeps behavior explicit and avoids "all rules" noise in daily testing.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add optional "apply to multiple sentences" batch mode in Studio (currently single-sentence apply for clarity).
  - Consider adding server-side aggregated endpoint to reduce client fan-out calls when many rules are selected.
## 2026-03-12 (Rules V2 Studio usability fixes)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` Studio view UX:
    - removed sentenceId display from sentence rows,
    - increased sentence text size for readability,
    - removed confusing secondary line (`translation`) from sentence list rows,
    - added auto-preview trigger when sentence/rule selection changes,
    - added empty-state hint when no preview/candidate result.
  - Normalized file encoding to UTF-8 without BOM and resolved hook/lint warnings.
- What was learned:
  - Operators expect selection to immediately show preview results; requiring manual preview click causes 閳ユ笜o result閿?confusion.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add an explicit toggle `Auto Preview On/Off` for very large rule sets.
## 2026-03-12 (Rules V2 Studio readability + non-match visibility)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx`:
    - sentence rows now show `ID: {sentenceId}` with neutral style,
    - sentence/rule/generated panels use larger text for readability,
    - preview logic now always shows per-selected-rule result rows (including non-match / no-candidate reasons) instead of blank panel,
    - cleaned Studio labels and empty-state guidance text.
- What was learned:
  - Empty preview panel is interpreted as failure by operators; explicit non-match rows are required for trust and debugging.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optionally add explicit `match-only` filter toggle in generated panel to hide unmatched rows when needed.
## 2026-03-12 (Rules V2 not-found root cause fix)
- What changed:
  - Backend compatibility fix in `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`:
    - preview/generate rule queries changed from strict `{ status: 'active', enabled: true }`
      to tolerant filters `{ status: { $ne: 'archived' }, enabled: { $ne: false } }`.
  - This allows legacy rules with missing `status/enabled` fields to be found by preview and candidate generation.
- What was learned:
  - Rule list and preview used inconsistent default semantics, causing "visible in list but not found in preview" failures.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional one-time data cleanup: backfill missing `status/enabled` on historical `RuleTemplate` docs.
## 2026-03-12 (Rules V2 generated exercise readability: question + answer)
- What changed:
  - Enhanced `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` Studio generated panel to render per-candidate details:
    - question prompt,
    - resolved answer (supports `correctAnswer`, `answer`, and cloze `gaps[].answers` fallback),
    - options list when present.
  - Added helper utilities `toStringArray()` and `resolveCandidateAnswer()` for robust payload parsing.
- What was learned:
  - Operators need review output in assessment form (question/answer/options), not only metadata and prompt summary.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add an "Edit draft payload" quick action for inline correction before candidate approval.

## 2026-03-12 (adaptive recommendation V1 in lesson flow)
- What changed:
  - Implemented backend adaptive learning production loop in `duoxx_server`:
    - Added models: `src/models/LearningAttempt.js`, `src/models/UserKnowledgeState.js`, `src/models/UserSnapshotState.js`, `src/models/LearningSession.js`.
    - Exported new models in `src/models/index.js`.
    - Added feature flags in `src/config/index.js`: `learning.adaptiveV1Enabled`, `learning.adaptiveV1RolloutPercent`.
    - Added service `src/services/adaptiveLearningService.js` with session start/submit/state logic, 80/20 candidate pools, scoring, no-repeat window, fallback chain, and knowledge/snapshot state updates.
    - Added tests `src/services/adaptiveLearningService.test.js`.
    - Extended learning routes in `src/routes/learning.js`:
      - `POST /api/learning/sessions/start`
      - `POST /api/learning/sessions/:sessionId/submit`
      - `GET /api/learning/sessions/:sessionId/state`
      - kept existing lesson endpoint for compatibility fallback.
  - Implemented frontend adaptive lesson integration in `duoxx`:
    - Extended API client `src/services/learningApi.ts` with adaptive session request/response types and methods.
    - Updated `app/lesson-exercise/[lessonId].tsx`:
      - logged-in users attempt adaptive session start and render `firstExercise`
      - local grading for `multiple_choice` and `fill_blank` before submit
      - submit to adaptive API and render returned `nextExercise`
      - explicit mastery feedback controls (`mastered`/`not_mastered`)
      - recommendation reason UI
      - runtime fallback to static lesson sequence when adaptive submit fails.
- What was learned:
  - Current project has unrelated global TypeScript errors, so full `tsc --noEmit` is not a reliable gate for this feature; targeted lint/tests are required per-change.
  - WSL backend tests must be run inside WSL path to avoid Windows UNC + `cross-env` execution failures.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add route-level integration tests for `/sessions/start|submit|state` happy path and 401/403/409 branches.
  - Add analytics dashboards for adaptive metrics (completion rate, repeat rate, API latency) aligned with rollout stages.
  - Decide default production values for `LEARNING_ADAPTIVE_V1_ENABLED` and rollout percentage before full user rollout.
- Addendum:
  - Added adaptive start-route tests in `duoxx_server/src/routes/learning.test.js` (401 + success path).
  - Added env defaults in `duoxx_server/.env.development` for adaptive rollout control.
## 2026-03-13 (V3 architecture reserve: tasks, prescriptions, learner capability)
- What changed:
  - Extended backend content/learning domain to reserve the V3 architecture:
    - Added models in `duoxx_server/src/models/`:
      - `KnowledgeNode.js`
      - `KnowledgeEdge.js`
      - `TaskBlueprint.js`
      - `LearningPrescription.js`
      - `UserCapabilityState.js`
      - `DocumentAsset.js`
      - `ParagraphAsset.js`
    - Extended existing models:
      - `SentenceAsset.js` now includes document/paragraph linkage, sequence, syntax frames, sentence pattern, knowledge node refs, scene tags, tags, quality status.
      - `ExerciseSnapshot.js` now reserves `true_false`, `primaryKnowledgeNodeId`, `knowledgeNodeIds`, `assetRefs`, `diagnosticRole`, `trainingMode`, `interactionMode`, `sceneTags`, `explanationNodeIds`, `qualityScore`.
      - `LearningSession.js` now includes `prescriptionId`, `sourceTaskId`, `entryType`, `entryId`.
    - Updated `duoxx_server/src/models/index.js` exports.
  - Extended backend services/routes:
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`:
      - sentence asset normalization upgraded to new schema
      - added `list/createKnowledgeNode`
      - added `getKnowledgeGraph`
      - added `list/createTaskBlueprint`
      - added `getCoverageOverview`
    - `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`:
      - added `/knowledge-nodes`
      - added `/knowledge-nodes/:nodeId/graph`
      - added `/task-blueprints`
      - added `/coverage/overview`
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/adaptiveLearningService.js`:
      - adaptive sessions now create `LearningPrescription`
      - added lightweight `UserCapabilityState` update on answer submit
      - added `getLatestPrescription()`
    - `duoxx_server/src/routes/learning.js`:
      - session start/state now return `prescriptionId`
      - added `/api/learning/prescriptions/latest`
      - added `/api/learning/tasks/blueprints`
      - `true_false` snapshots now map to renderable multiple-choice output
  - Extended frontend API and entry scaffolding:
    - `duoxx/src/services/learningApi.ts`:
      - added `LearningPrescriptionSummary`
      - added `TaskBlueprintSummary`
      - added `getLatestPrescription()`
      - added `getTaskBlueprints()`
    - `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`:
      - extended `SentenceAsset`
      - added `KnowledgeNode`, `KnowledgeEdge`, `KnowledgeGraphResponse`, `TaskBlueprint`, `CoverageOverview`
      - added knowledge/task/coverage API methods
    - `duoxx/app/(tabs)/index.tsx`:
      - added new top-level growth entry cards:
        - `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹鎷囬敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熺禇
        - `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熺潾闈╂嫹`
        - `閿熸枻鎷峰閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹璁敓鏂ゆ嫹`
    - Added new pages:
      - `duoxx/app/prescriptions.tsx`
      - `duoxx/app/weakness-workbench.tsx`
      - `duoxx/app/task-training.tsx`
- What was learned:
  - The safest upgrade path is not replacing the current adaptive service, but layering `Prescription` and `CapabilityState` onto it so lesson-based flow still works.
  - `KnowledgeNode` must serve both retrieval and explanation/navigation, so it cannot stay as a flat tag list.
  - Reserving `trainingMode` and `interactionMode` now avoids a later hard break when exercises move from recognition-only into output/conversation tasks.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Wire admin `/admin/pipeline` UI to the new `Knowledge / Tasks / Coverage` APIs.
  - Add first real `TaskBlueprint` seed data and connect task entry to session start beyond lesson-only mode.
  - Build a unified frontend knowledge detail container that uses graph traversal instead of per-component explanation payloads.
## 2026-03-13 (V3 admin UI follow-up: Architecture Workbench)
- What changed:
  - Added `duoxx/components/admin/ArchitectureWorkbench.tsx` as a new admin workbench for V3 reserve layers.
  - The workbench provides 3 flat operational views:
    - `Knowledge`: list/create knowledge nodes, inspect graph preview.
    - `Tasks`: list/create task blueprints, inspect task detail.
    - `Coverage`: query snapshot coverage by knowledge node / task / scene tag.
  - Integrated the new workbench into `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` via a new header entry button `Architecture` and a dedicated fullscreen modal, parallel to existing `Rules V2`.
- What was learned:
  - `/admin/pipeline` should expose new architecture layers in independent workbenches instead of mixing them into the already-dense course content table.
  - For this stage, flat lists + create forms + graph/coverage inspection are enough; a visual graph editor would add complexity before the graph model is fully operationalized.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Connect `KnowledgeNode` selection in exercise review and explanation flows.
  - Add `TaskBlueprint -> start training` bridge once session start supports task entry directly.
  - Add coverage drill-down from aggregated counts to specific `ExerciseSnapshot` rows.
## 2026-03-13 (candidate review chain upgraded with knowledge node metadata)
- What changed:
  - Extended backend `ExerciseCandidate` in `duoxx_server/src/models/ExerciseCandidate.js` with:
    - `primaryKnowledgeNodeId`
    - `knowledgeNodeIds[]`
    - `diagnosticRole`
    - `trainingMode`
    - `interactionMode`
    - `sceneTags[]`
  - Extended `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`:
    - candidate generation now seeds review metadata from `SentenceAsset` + exercise type defaults
    - candidate patch API now supports updating knowledge/training metadata
    - candidate approval now persists these fields into `ExerciseSnapshot`
    - approved snapshot now writes:
      - `primaryKnowledgeNodeId`
      - `knowledgeNodeIds[]`
      - `assetRefs`
      - `diagnosticRole`
      - `trainingMode`
      - `interactionMode`
      - `sceneTags[]`
      - `qualityScore`
  - Extended `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js` candidate patch route to accept the new metadata fields.
  - Extended frontend `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts` candidate types and update payload.
  - Upgraded `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` candidate review tab:
    - added candidate review editor
    - operator can now edit prompt / explanation / answers / options
    - operator can now assign `primaryKnowledgeNodeId`, `knowledgeNodeIds`, `diagnosticRole`, `trainingMode`, `interactionMode`, `sceneTags`
    - candidate rows now expose `Edit` before `Approve/Reject`
- What was learned:
  - Knowledge graph and coverage APIs are not enough by themselves; candidate approval is the real seam where graph metadata must enter the formal snapshot pool.
  - Default training profiles can be derived safely from current exercise type (`cloze`, `multiple_choice`, `true_false`) without blocking future richer task modes.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Replace free-text role/mode inputs in candidate editor with constrained pickers for safer operator UX.
  - Surface `knowledgeNodeIds` and `diagnosticRole` directly in lesson/exercise analytics and coverage drill-down.
  - Add backend tests for candidate patch/approve persistence of new snapshot metadata.
## 2026-03-13 (coverage drill-down + constrained candidate metadata editor)
- What changed:
  - Extended backend pipeline service/routes for snapshot drill-down:
    - `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js` added `listExerciseSnapshots()` with filters:
      - `knowledgeNodeId`
      - `taskId`
      - `sceneTag`
      - `status`
    - `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js` added `GET /api/pipeline/exercise-snapshots`.
  - Extended frontend pipeline API in `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`:
    - added `ExerciseSnapshotSummary`
    - added `listExerciseSnapshots()`.
  - Upgraded `duoxx/components/admin/ArchitectureWorkbench.tsx` coverage tab:
    - coverage query now loads both aggregate distributions and matching snapshot rows
    - added `Matched Snapshots` panel for operational drill-down from aggregate coverage to concrete published exercises.
  - Upgraded `duoxx/components/admin/RuleTemplateWorkbench.tsx` candidate editor UX:
    - replaced free-text editing for `diagnosticRole`, `trainingMode`, `interactionMode` with constrained selector rows (pill buttons)
    - keeps operator freedom where needed, but prevents malformed enum values from entering formal snapshots.
- What was learned:
  - Coverage without drill-down is not enough for operators; they need to see which exact snapshots satisfy or miss a filter.
  - The highest-risk review metadata should use constrained UI, not raw text inputs, otherwise the formal snapshot pool degrades quickly.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add `Matched Snapshots -> open in course/lesson context` deep links.
  - Replace free-text taskType/nodeType creation fields with constrained selectors as well.
  - Add route/service tests for `GET /api/pipeline/exercise-snapshots` filtering semantics.
## 2026-03-13 (admin workbench follow-up)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/components/admin/ArchitectureWorkbench.tsx`: constrained `KnowledgeNode.nodeType` and `TaskBlueprint.taskType` to fixed selectors; added `Open Course Context` action from Coverage snapshot rows.

- Learned:
  - Coverage drill-down is materially more useful when operators can jump straight from a snapshot row back to the owning course context.
  - Workbench creation forms should use constrained enums instead of free text; otherwise metadata quality degrades quickly.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add direct snapshot management view in `/admin/pipeline` instead of relying only on candidate approval and coverage drill-down.
  - Add editable graph edges for `KnowledgeNode` so knowledge navigation is not read-only.
## 2026-03-13 (snapshot workbench)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/components/admin/ArchitectureWorkbench.tsx`: added `Snapshots` tab for direct published snapshot operations; supports search/filter, detail view, metadata editing, archive/reactivate, and course-context jump.
  - `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`: extended snapshot list filters and payload fields; added `updateExerciseSnapshot` client.
  - `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`: extended snapshot listing filters and fields; added snapshot update service for prompt/explanation/knowledge/training/status metadata.
  - `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`: added `PATCH /api/pipeline/exercise-snapshots/:snapshotId` and expanded snapshot list query support.
- Learned:
  - Published snapshot management needs to live beside coverage, not behind candidate review only; operators need direct archive/reactivate and metadata fixes on the final pool.
  - Snapshot search must include prompt/course/lesson/snapshotId to be operationally usable.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add dedicated snapshot option/answer editor for multiple-choice and true/false payloads.
  - Add graph-edge editing in `Knowledge` so node graph is not read-only.
## 2026-03-13 (task session + graph edges + snapshot payload editor)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/app/task-training.tsx`: cleaned text encoding and added direct task start CTA; task training now routes into the shared exercise screen and is gated for logged-in users.

  - `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`: added knowledge-edge CRUD clients and expanded snapshot update payload.

  - `duoxx_server/src/services/contentPipelineService.js`: added knowledge-edge CRUD service methods and snapshot update support for options/correctAnswer.
  - `duoxx_server/src/routes/pipeline.js`: added knowledge-edge routes and expanded snapshot update route payload.
  - `duoxx_server/src/routes/learning.test.js`: added task-session route coverage.
- Learned:
  - Task training can reuse the same exercise renderer if session bootstrap is generalized; the real split is session context, not screen UI.
  - Snapshot operations need two layers: metadata editing for all snapshots and payload editing only for choice-based snapshots; cloze gap truth still belongs upstream.
  - Knowledge graph editing becomes operationally useful once the operator can create and archive edges directly from the selected node context.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add upstream cloze gap editor based on sentence tokens rather than editing snapshot payload directly.
  - Add task start CTA inside admin `Tasks` workbench as a preview/debug path for operators.
  - Add snapshot revision history or stale markers when upstream assets change and published snapshots need re-review.

## 2026-03-17 (operator import whitelist v1)
- What changed:
  - Rebuilt `duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx` into a stable flat workbench after the previous file became partially corrupted and syntactically unsafe.
  - Import tab now uses `upload -> immediate parse/preview -> row edit -> template select -> generate draft -> publish` instead of empty manual Step 2 / Step 3 clicks.
  - Import UI now supports whitelist-first source handling:
    - `word_knowledge_csv`
    - `sentence_asset_csv`
    - markdown/txt structured course fallback
  - Added row-level parsed source preview and editor for word/sentence rows, row selection, filtered template selection, local draft generation, draft save, and publish fallback.
  - Preserved review workflows in the same workbench for:
    - knowledge nodes
    - exercise candidates
    - task blueprints
  - Verified current import pipeline files with lint and kept admin import parser tests green.
- What was learned:
  - The earlier step-based import UI failed because it exposed internal parse stages instead of operator intent; operators need immediate visibility into parsed source rows.
  - The clean boundary is: source preview first, generation template second, draft third.
  - `OperatorWorkbench.tsx` had accumulated encoding and structure damage; replacing the component root-to-leaf was lower risk than trying to keep patching it.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add row-level delete/add actions in import preview so operators can finish source correction without leaving the workbench.
  - Add explicit unsupported-CSV diagnostics panel that lists missing required headers for each whitelist protocol.
  - Consider moving markdown/txt draft conversion into `adminImportWizard.ts` so the component stops owning that conversion logic.
- Follow-up:
  - Improved unsupported CSV diagnosis in import UI.
  - Validation now exposes actual headers, missing required headers for both whitelist protocols, legacy knowledge-block hint, and first raw file lines for quick operator debugging.

## 2026-03-18 (jsx unicode text rendering fix)
- Changed files + intent:
  - duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx: fixed import-tab label rendering where literal \uXXXX sequences were displayed to users; switched affected JSX text nodes to expression strings (e.g. {'\\u6587...'}) so React decodes unicode escapes correctly at runtime.
- Learned:
  - In JSX text nodes, \uXXXX is not interpreted; unicode escapes must be inside JavaScript string expressions or replaced by actual UTF-8 literals.
## 2026-03-18 (import word v3: sense/example model + single-page review editor)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/src/services/adminImportWizard.ts`: upgraded `word_knowledge_csv` parsing from single-value rows to `word + senses[] + examples[]` model; added multi-value protocol (`|| / ;; / |`), sense/example-level validation localization (`rowNumber/senseIndex/exampleIndex`), template availability gating by row capability, legacy single-value word protocol hard block (`LEGACY_WORD_PROTOCOL_BLOCKED`), and word exercise generation by sense/example with metadata (`senseIndex/exampleIndex`).
  - `duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx`: updated Word CSV template to v3 protocol, changed required-header diagnostics to `word + translationZh`, and refactored import row editor to structured word editing (word base fields + per-sense + per-example edit/add/remove) with immediate re-parse/re-validation on every change.
  - `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/adminImportWizard.test.ts`: replaced word import tests with v3 coverage (multi-sense parse, legacy protocol block, sense/example mismatch localization, template gating, cloze generation metadata).
  - `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`: extended `ImportValidationIssue` with optional `rowNumber/senseIndex/exampleIndex` to carry fine-grained import error location.
  - `duoxx/docs/import-word-v3-contract.md`: added backend contract checklist for preview payload shape, v3 CSV rules, validation localization, and publish audit `protocolVersion`.
- Learned:
  - Word import needs sense-aware structure as source truth; otherwise multi-POS/multi-example data always collapses into lossy single-value patches.
  - Template visibility must be data-capability-driven (sentence templates require anchored examples), not source-kind-only.
  - Running Jest in this environment requires `--runInBand` due worker spawn permission (`EPERM`).
- Verification:
  - `cmd /c npx eslint components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx src/services/adminImportWizard.ts src/services/__tests__/adminImportWizard.test.ts src/services/pipelineApi.ts` passed.
  - `cmd /c npm test -- src/services/__tests__/adminImportWizard.test.ts --runInBand` passed (13/13).
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Backend `import-jobs` routes need to adopt the same v3 preview payload and validation fields for full end-to-end parity.
  - Import UI can further add inline 閳ユ笍ump to first blocking issue閿?and row-level issue filtering for large files.

## 2026-03-18 (V4 asset package API bridge + backend-first import panel)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/src/services/pipelineApi.ts`: added V4 asset-package client methods for `create/standardize/preview/patch/validate/publish/generate-course-draft`.

- Learned:
  - The earlier `pipelineApi.ts` failure was caused by PowerShell replacement swallowing template-literal backticks, which broke every generated endpoint path after insertion.
  - For this repo, whole-file rewrite is safer than incremental patching once JSX + encoding corruption starts; targeted `tsc` filtering is a more reliable verification gate than repo ESLint commands that depend on local/global config state.

## 2026-03-19 (V4 slot validation + parse-gated review)

  - `duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx`: refined the V4 import flow so global `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷锋牎閿熸枻鎷穈 only appears after `閿熸枻鎷峰閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`; moved each CSV template button into its own upload slot; slot badges now switch from `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹/閿熸枻鎷烽€塦 to `閿熸枻鎷烽敓杈冭揪鎷?閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`; per-slot header errors are shown immediately after file selection; fixed slot inspection call order and parse-state reset behavior.

- Learned:
  - The screenshoted `SENSE_HEADERS_INVALID` root cause was not parser randomness; it came from allowing a file with `examples` shape to be placed into the `senses` slot and only catching it later during package parse.

  - Run a browser smoke pass on `/admin/pipeline` to verify the new slot-level error UX and badge transitions on real uploads.
  - Consider adding file-name mismatch warnings when a known `examples.csv` filename is intentionally placed into the `senses` slot, even if the user clicks that slot manually.
## 2026-03-19 (V4 upload slots: immediate file checks + parse-gated validation)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx`: changed V4 slot behavior so file-level feedback happens immediately on upload, while the global `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷锋牎閿熸枻鎷穈 section stays hidden until `閿熸枻鎷峰閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`; moved each CSV template button into its corresponding upload slot; changed slot badges from `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹/閿熸枻鎷烽€塦 to runtime state (`閿熸枻鎷烽敓杈冭揪鎷穈 / `閿熷彨杈炬嫹閿熸枻鎷穈) after selection; reset stale parse preview state when files change.

  - `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/lexicalAssetImport.test.ts`: added coverage for immediate slot inspection and forced-slot wrong-file detection.
- Learned:
  - There are two distinct validation layers in V4 and they must stay visually separate: upload-time slot inspection (cheap, local, per file) and parse-time package validation (cross-file, entry/sense/example graph aware).
  - The screenshot root cause is mostly UX, not parser correctness: when a user drops `examples.csv` into the `senses` slot, the current parser correctly reports `SENSE_HEADERS_INVALID`, but the UI previously delayed useful feedback and kept misleading `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹` badges.

  - The right-pane review surface needs two levels of information only: word-level lexical facets and sense-level meaning/examples; repeating lemma/headword metadata in multiple places makes the page feel larger without adding information.
  - If future rendering dimensions are expected, they must enter through the standard asset contract first; UI-only placeholders create false completeness.
- Verification:
  - `cmd /c .\duoxx\node_modules\.bin\tsc -p duoxx\tsconfig.json --noEmit --pretty false 2>&1 | findstr /I /C:"LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx" /C:"lexicalAssetImport.ts" /C:"lexicalAssetImport.test.ts" /C:"adminLexicalAssetV4.ts"` produced no matched errors for touched files.
  - `cmd /c npm --prefix duoxx test -- src/services/__tests__/lexicalAssetImport.test.ts --runInBand` passed (11/11).
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Run a browser smoke pass to verify the flattened word-level facets section still reads compactly on real web width.
  - Consider whether `phrases/collocations/idioms/slang/spokenExpressions` should later move from entry metadata into first-class assets when cross-linking and recommendation need stronger structure.
## 2026-03-19 (V5 single-file lexical import)
- Changed files + intent:
  - `duoxx/src/services/lexicalSingleFileImport.ts`: introduced a new single-file lexical asset parser that accepts Markdown as the primary protocol and TXT/CSV as compatible inputs, then normalizes them into a human-readable review model (`word -> senses -> examples -> facets`) instead of exposing technical entry/sense/example objects.
  - `duoxx/src/config/adminLexicalSingleFile.ts`: added the V5 operator copy plus official single-file templates for Markdown, TXT, and CSV long-table import.
  - `duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx`: rewrote the import panel into a single upload-and-review page; auto-parse on upload, hide internal ids/JSONL/downstream actions, show word list on the left and grouped word/sense/example/facet review on the right, and surface only human-readable validation messages.
  - `duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx`: removed the old V4/legacy course import branch from the default Import tab so Review Hub now exposes only the new single-file lexical import flow.
  - `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/lexicalSingleFileImport.test.ts`: added parser coverage for Markdown, TXT, CSV aggregation, missing CSV headers, and missing-example validation.
- Learned:
  - The operator review unit is `one word and everything under it`; any UI that exposes `entries/senses/examples` as first-class visible columns becomes technical and hard to use.
  - For this admin flow, the correct simplification is not 閳ユ竾ewer buttons on the same data model閿?but 閳ユ笝ne upload contract + one review shape + no downstream generation in the main page.閿?- Verification:

- What was learned:
  - The cleanest V2 boundary is: templates carry knowledge only; exercises are system-generated around a sense.

  - A direct Node `require` check confirmed `duoxx_server/src/services/lexicalQuizService.js` still exports a callable `generateQuizVersions`.

## 2026-03-20 (Lexical practice answer-validation investigation)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/src/services/lexicalQuizLessonAdapter.ts` to normalize translation-choice options on read:
    - legacy `word_card` distractors now ignore non-Chinese answers such as `true/false`
    - translation-like options are deterministically rotated so the correct answer is not always in slot A
  - Updated `duoxx/src/storage/lexicalQuizReviewStorage.ts` so newly generated `translation_choice` questions are stored with rotated option order.
  - Updated backend generation in `duoxx_server/src/services/lexicalQuizService.js` so Mongo-generated `translation_choice` questions use the same rotated option order.
  - Expanded `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/lexicalQuizLessonAdapter.test.ts` with:
    - legacy distractor pollution regression coverage
    - explicit wrong-answer-must-fail coverage
  - Updated `duoxx/src/storage/__tests__/lexicalQuizReviewStorage.test.ts` to assert generated translation-choice options are no longer answer-first.
- What was learned:
  - The user-reported 閿熸枻鎷穉ll answers are correct閿熸枻鎷?symptom was not reproducible in the learner screen; browser verification showed wrong answers still fail.
  - The real root causes were stale lexical option construction rules: polluted legacy distractors and overly predictable answer placement.
  - Active legacy `word_card` rows already stored in Mongo can still be read safely because the learner adapter now normalizes them at runtime.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Decide whether to run a one-off migration for existing Mongo `translation_choice` / promoted legacy `word_card` records so review-side stored options also match the new order.

## 2026-03-20 (translation-choice distractor quality upgrade)
- What changed:
  - Tightened `duoxx_server/src/services/lexicalQuizService.js` and `duoxx/src/storage/lexicalQuizReviewStorage.ts` so translation-choice distractors are now ranked by same part of speech, difficulty proximity, and scene-tag overlap.
  - Filtered distractors to translation-like Chinese text only; ASCII-only `true/false` style values are excluded from translation-choice pools.
  - Added backend and local-storage tests that verify the higher-quality distractor selection path.
- What was learned:
  - The generator can stay simple at the API boundary while still producing better questions by scoring candidates before option rotation.
  - Keeping the backend and local fallback aligned avoids a split-brain quiz experience when the API is unavailable.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - If older stored quiz rows should be rewritten too, add a separate data cleanup later; do not mix that with the generator rule change.

- What changed:
  - Added responsive compact-mode logic in `duoxx/app/(tabs)/index.tsx` using `useWindowDimensions` with threshold `width < 390`.
  - In compact mode, diagnostic summary cards and diagnostic action buttons switch to stacked vertical layout for readability.
  - Added compact spacing variants for section paddings, headers, avatar/hearts blocks, and quick-start area.
  - Child/student avatar size now scales from `large` to `medium` on compact screens.
  - Heart icon size now adapts (`24` -> `22`) for tighter but clear display in compact mode.
- What was learned:
  - The three-section IA works better when narrow-screen layout is explicitly handled; relying on default flex row compression creates readability loss in diagnostic cards.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Validate visual balance on 360/375 width devices in both adult and child modes.
  - Decide whether compact mode should also hide secondary subtitles in resource cards for even faster scanning.
## 2026-03-26 (Home tab minimal IA + deferred entry registry)
- What changed:
  - Rebuilt `duoxx/app/(tabs)/index.tsx` non-parent home into a minimal IA with only 3 visible primary blocks: `瀛︿範閿熸枻鎷风煡璇嗛敓鏂ゆ嫹AI閿熺嫛纭锋嫹閿熸枻鎷穈, `閿熸枻鎷蜂範閿熸枻鎷风煡璇哷, and `灞曢敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`.

  - Added a preserved secondary-entry registry in code (`moreCards`) for routes that were previously visible but now intentionally deferred behind `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`.
- What was learned:
  - The previous layout overload came from exposing too many same-priority actions at once; moving secondary actions behind one controlled expansion keeps clarity while retaining capability.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Validate whether learners still discover `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹璁敓鏂ゆ嫹` and `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹閿熺潾闈╂嫹` at expected rates after moving them behind `閿熸枻鎷烽敓鏂ゆ嫹`.

- What was learned:
  - Most blocking failures came from barrel export collisions and route-file drift, not deep logic bugs.
  - Keeping route files physically present in `app/modules/*` is required for Expo Router typed-route stability.
  - Dynamic optional dependencies like `expo-speech` need explicit lint handling when not guaranteed in all environments.

  - `cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit` -> pass.
  - `npm run lint` -> `0 errors, 248 warnings`.
- Next steps / open questions:
