## 2026-03-27 (Lint warning burndown to zero + stability verification)
- What changed:
  - Cleared remaining lint warnings across hook deps, unused imports/vars, and test typing in:
    - `duoxx/app/error-detail.tsx`
    - `duoxx/app/scene-course/[sceneId].tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/components/celebration/CelebrationScreen.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/components/feedback/AchievementToast.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/components/feedback/MilestoneModal.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/dynamic-lexicon/components/AchievementBadges.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/dynamic-lexicon/components/ChunkExercise.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/dynamic-lexicon/components/VocabMeter.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/dynamic-lexicon/screens/DynamicLexiconScreen.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/imperfect-dialogue/components/DialogueAvatarDemo.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/speaking-avatar/components/SpeakingAvatarView.tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/survival-phrases/screens/SurvivalPhrasesScreen.tsx`
    - plus targeted test files under `speaking-avatar`, `imperfect-dialogue`, `survival-phrases`.
  - Resolved two runtime parser breakages caused by malformed text literals in:
    - `duoxx/app/modules/listening-speaking/[unitId].tsx`
    - `duoxx/src/modules/dynamic-lexicon/components/ChunkExercise.tsx`
  - Updated test mocks to avoid Jest hoist/TDZ failures by inlining `Animated.Value` mock classes inside `jest.mock` factories.
- What was learned:
  - A large portion of residual warnings came from hook-deps rules on mount-only animation/setup effects; handling needed either dependency-complete callbacks or explicit lint intent comments.
  - When files contain mixed/legacy encoded literals, small line edits can accidentally introduce unterminated JSX/text nodes; lint + parser checks are the fastest safety net.
  - Jest mock hoisting can break top-level class references inside `jest.mock` factories; embedding mock classes inside the factory is the most robust pattern.
- Verification:
  - `cmd /c npm run lint` -> pass (0 warnings, 0 errors).
  - `cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit` -> pass.
  - `cmd /c npx jest ... --runInBand` (4 targeted suites) -> pass.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Run a broader learner-flow smoke path (home -> module -> submit -> feedback) and admin pipeline smoke path to catch any UI text/encoding regressions not covered by tests.

    - resilient review-state hydration (defensive normalization, no `undefined.length` crash path)
    - auto-first import flow: create batch -> load report/candidates -> auto-publish when no pending reviews
    - minimal manual review actions for candidates: `闁俺绻?/ 閹锋帞绮?/ 閸氬牆鑻焋

    - click expansion item to promote to main node and continue expanding
    - supports group filters, one-step back, and return-to-root

    - `duoxx/src/modules/vocab-recognition/screens/VocabExerciseScreen.tsx`: corrected end-of-session param race when quick-marking `閻旂喐鍊?閹哄本褰檂
    - `duoxx/src/modules/vocab-recognition/screens/VocabCompleteScreen.tsx`: switched to composite score (`0.65*accuracy + 0.35*masteryProgress`) and updated result messaging.

  - The 閳ユ粎鐡熼柨娆掔窛婢舵矮绲鹃弽鍥唶閹哄本褰欐潏鍐樋娴犲秶绮扮拹鐔锋倻閺傚洦顢嶉垾?problem came from both scoring strategy and final-route state race; only changing copy is insufficient.
  - Admin import panel reliability depends on strict data normalization for restored local session payloads, not only parser correctness.
  - Auto-publish can be safely triggered only when pending-review candidates are zero; otherwise strict gate + tri-action review remains necessary.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add explicit API typings for `lexiconApi` responses to reduce `any`-style casts in UI.

    - import batch from review payload
    - strict gate publish blocked while `pending_review` candidate exists
    - approve candidate -> report becomes `ready_to_publish`
    - publish creates active snapshot
    - learner service read path works on persisted snapshot (`getNode`, `expandNode`, `markUserNodeState`, `getRecommendations`)
- What was learned:
  - The strict gate behavior is sensitive to unresolved pending candidates; this must be validated against persisted collections, not only mocked route state.
  - `getRecommendations` may return `new` ahead of `mastered_not_due` in mixed-root scenarios; assertions should check containment rather than fixed first-position reason.

  - Updated `duoxx_server_link/src/models/GeneratedQuizVersion.js` to remove `scheduled_refresh` from `generationReason` enum.
  - Added explicit policy line in `duoxx/docs/lexical-quiz-lifecycle-v1.md`: import/publish are human-triggered, no timed/scheduled auto-publish.
- What was learned:
  - In current codebase, the concrete violation of manual-trigger policy was UI-side auto publish, not backend route logic.
  - PowerShell re-encoding on this file can easily break mojibake-heavy strings; compile/lint checks are mandatory right after edit.
- Verification:
  - Frontend:
    - `cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false` (duoxx) -> pass
    - `cmd /c npx eslint components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx --max-warnings=0` (duoxx) -> pass
  - Backend:
    - `npm test -- src/routes/pipeline.test.js src/routes/learning.test.js --runInBand` (duoxx_server_link) -> pass (2 suites / 14 tests)
  - Search guard:
    - `git grep -n "scheduled_refresh" -- src` (duoxx_server_link) -> no matches
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Keep staging observation for legacy compatibility endpoint usage, then proceed with phased retirement plan.

## 2026-04-03 (System test baseline step #1 executed, with environment blockers captured)
- What changed:
  - Executed baseline automation checks for current graph-first stack:
    - frontend type gate: `cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false` (duoxx) -> pass.
    - backend stable route suites: `src/routes/pipeline.test.js`, `src/routes/learning.test.js`, `src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js` -> pass.

    - `src/routes/lexiconGraph.e2e.test.js`
    - `src/services/__tests__/lexiconGraphService.integration.test.js`
    these failed due to `mongodb-memory-server` binary download/lockfile contention, not logic assertions.
  - Attempted authenticated HTTP smoke script against `http://localhost:3000`; blocked by register/index issue:
    - `/api/auth/register` returns `E11000 duplicate key ... email_1/phone_1 ... null`.
    - cannot create a new smoke user from this shell session without existing credentials.
- What was learned:
  - Current backend test matrix can be split into:
    - stable route-level suites (reliable baseline signal),
    - heavy mongodb-memory-server suites (sensitive to local binary cache/lock state).
  - Running environment still contains auth registration behavior coupled with null unique index constraints, which blocks credential bootstrap for automated smoke.
  - For system-level staging verification, having a fixed reusable operator test account is operationally safer than per-run account registration.
- Verification:
  - Pass:
    - `cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false` (duoxx)
    - `.\\node_modules\\.bin\\jest.cmd src/routes/pipeline.test.js src/routes/learning.test.js src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js --runInBand` (duoxx_server_link)
  - Blocked/fail evidence:
    - e2e/integration suites timed out in hooks while `mongodb-memory-server` was downloading `8.2.1` and contending on lockfile `C:\\Users\\Administrator\\.cache\\mongodb-binaries\\8.2.1.lock`.
    - auth smoke bootstrap failed with `E11000 duplicate key ... { email: null }` and `{ phone: null }`.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Unblock authenticated smoke with one reusable staging admin/operator account (or fix register null-unique path in running backend).
  - Resolve mongodb-memory-server cache lock/download state, then rerun the two deep suites to close baseline gate.

  - Therefore: architecture is graph-first in default path, but not yet safe for hard removal of compatibility endpoints.

    - `duoxx/app/lesson-exercise/[lessonId].tsx` (legacy learner quiz fetch)
    - `duoxx/components/admin/LexicalQuizReviewPanel.tsx` (legacy operator review actions)

## 2026-04-03 (asset governance toolchain v1 implemented)
- What changed:
  - Added `duoxx/src/services/assetLinkGovernance.ts` with four governance capabilities:
    - strict file-level contract report
    - canonical registry generation
    - unresolved label aggregation
    - patch suggestion generation (`add_alias/add_ref/create_node`)
  - Added unit test: `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/assetLinkGovernance.test.ts`.
  - Added rehearsal/integration test: `duoxx/src/services/__tests__/assetLinkGovernanceRehearsal.test.ts` (emits `[asset-link-governance]` JSON).
  - Upgraded `asset-link-enricher` script to run 3 test stages (rehearsal + diagnostics + governance) with per-stage exit-code checks and governance summary print.
  - Upgraded skill docs to include governance outputs; mirrored updates to both `.agents` and `.codex` paths.
  - Refreshed `reports/asset-link-baseline.json` with new `governance` payload.
- What was learned:
  - Governance report confirms two hard source-contract failures remain: `word.md` and `sentencePatterns.md`.
  - Distinct canonical keys are currently low (38), and most unresolved labels can be converted into explicit refs suggestions (`add_ref` dominates).
  - Script reliability improved by checking each jest invocation exit code independently (previously only last command status was effectively guarded).
- Verification:
  - `npm test -- src/services/__tests__/assetLinkGovernance.test.ts --runInBand` -> pass.
  - `npm test -- src/services/__tests__/assetLinkGovernanceRehearsal.test.ts --runInBand` -> pass.
  - `powershell -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File .\.agents\skills\asset-link-enricher\scripts\run-asset-link-enricher.ps1 -OutFile .\reports\asset-link-baseline.json` -> pass.
  - `npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false` -> pass.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Start repair batch #1 focused on source assets only:
    - normalize `sentencePatterns.md` into parser-compatible key-value blocks
    - resolve `word.md` unresolved top labels via explicit refs/aliases or adding missing canonical entries.

## 2026-04-03 (asset repair batch #1 finished)
- What changed:
  - Source assets were repaired directly (no frontend fallback):
    - `asserts/sentencePatterns.md`: rewritten into parser-friendly key-value blocks.
    - `asserts/word.md`: removed level comments, normalized merged-line artifacts, and added missing core entries.
    - `asserts/spokenExpressions.md`: normalized to strict line-mode format (`anchor (Lx): expression || zh`).
    - Expanded high-frequency unresolved targets in:
      - `asserts/phrases.md`
      - `asserts/collocations.md`
      - `asserts/slang.md`
      - `asserts/idioms.md`
  - Refreshed baseline report via skill script:
    - `reports/asset-link-baseline.json`.
- What was learned:
  - The biggest parser-quality gains came from format normalization (line-splitting and strict file-format conformance), not from frontend logic changes.
  - `word.md` still dominates unresolved volume, but contract gate is now clean across all 7 files.
- Verification:
  - `npm test -- src/services/__tests__/assetParseDiagnostics.test.ts --runInBand` -> pass.
  - `npm test -- src/services/__tests__/lexiconAssetsBundleRehearsal.test.ts --runInBand` -> pass.

## 2026-04-07 (System-wide UX/Feature evaluation, no code changes)
- What changed:

  - Reviewed key flows: home entry, courses, lesson exercise, knowledge absorb 2.0, profile/progress/error book, and pipeline operations.
  - Built evaluation baseline via `ui-ux-pro-max` design-system + ux + react-native stack guidance.
- What was learned:
  - Feature coverage is broad, but interaction consistency and information architecture are still uneven between learner and admin surfaces.
  - Accessibility metadata is currently missing in interactive components (`accessibilityRole/Label/Hint` global scan count = 0).
  - Some screens still use placeholder user IDs (`default-user`, `user-123`), which reduces data trust and UX coherence.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Define one unified interaction spec (navigation hierarchy, action priority, component language) for learner and admin separately.
  - Land an accessibility baseline pass (roles, labels, focus order, touch target policy).
  - Replace hardcoded user IDs with auth-bound identity in all user-facing analytics/progress screens.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge Absorb relevance fix: synonym/antonym noise reduction)
- What changed:
  - Updated duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts.
  - Tightened allowed node kinds for synonyms and ntonyms from ['word','phrase'] to ['word'].
  - Added precision-first early return for synonym/antonym resolution: only direct curated facet links are used; keyword-based fallback recall is skipped.
- Root cause learned:
  - Near-synonym/antonym group was polluted by keyword fallback (elatedTermIndex) and phrase-allowed kinds, so unrelated phrase-like entries could appear.
- Verification:
  - cmd /c npx eslint "src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts" "app/knowledge-absorb.tsx" -> pass.
  - cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false -> pass.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add a small 鈥滄暟鎹笉瓒斥€?empty hint when direct curated synonyms/antonyms are absent, instead of recalling noisy semantic neighbors.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge Absorb strict-direct mode for expansion relevance)
- What changed:
  - Updated duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts:
    - Added strictDirect?: boolean to esolveExpansionNodeRefs.
    - When strictDirect is true, expansion resolution returns only direct curated relations from entryExpansionMap, skipping keyword fallback recall.
  - Updated duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx:
    - Expansion fetch now calls esolveExpansionNodeRefs(..., strictDirect: true) for absorb screen.
    - Removed UI-side hard truncation (slice(0, 16)), so group shows full direct relation set.
    - Increased fetch limit to avoid hidden direct items.
- Root cause learned:
  - Unrelated phrase-heavy items were introduced by keyword fallback recall path; this is useful for discovery but harms precision for absorb-card expansion semantics.
- Verification:
  - cmd /c npx eslint "app/knowledge-absorb.tsx" "src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts" -> pass.
  - cmd /c npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false -> pass.

  - Added vertical paged group switching for non-sentence expansion content (one group per page) with momentum index sync to active group state.
  - Simplified swipe affordance to a compact hint badge and switched expansion item rendering to column rows.
  - Kept sentence insight module tab behavior intact while sharing the same expansion container.
- What was learned:
  - Keeping only one vertical gesture source (group pager) avoids nested-scroll conflicts on mobile and makes the interaction predictable.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add page dots for group position awareness if users still miss the swipe interaction.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb: expansion relevance + layout correction)
- What changed:
  - Updated duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx layout so expansion area is inside active workspace, directly under the word card, and consumes remaining height.
  - Made the word card region scrollable/shrinkable to prevent expansion area from collapsing to a single visible row.
  - Flattened expansion visual layers by removing inner bordered wrapper style (avoids big-border-inside-big-border).
  - Reduced expansion module request limit from 12 to 8 for denser relevance.
  - Updated duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts recall policy:
    - direct facet links are preferred and returned first when present;
    - keyword recall is only used when direct links are absent;
    - recall candidates are scope-filtered to same entry or same active sense.
- What was learned:
  - Precision loss mainly came from unrestricted keyword recall; restricting recall scope and preferring curated links improves relevance substantially.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add a small telemetry counter for empty pages per group to further tune recall thresholds.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb: position rollback unified)
- What changed:
  - Restored expansion card positioning to the agreed stable layout: top content section first, expansion card anchored below it, and action buttons at the bottom in a consistent slot.
  - Reverted the temporary card-internal placement shift that caused perceived position drift.
  - Kept prior non-position fixes intact: no inner nested border shell in expansion content and improved relevance filtering in resolveExpansionNodeRefs.
- What was learned:
  - Position consistency matters more than local layout experiments in this page; structure changes should be opt-in and isolated.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: if needed, lock explicit min/max heights for top section vs expansion area to guarantee deterministic visual ratios across devices.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb spacing hotfix: card-to-expansion gap)
- What changed:
  - In duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx, removed flex growth from topSection and activeWorkspace.
  - This makes the top word card area size to content instead of stretching, so expansion card now attaches directly below without large empty gap.
- What was learned:
  - Keeping top content containers as flex:1 can introduce false vertical whitespace when bottom region is also flex-driven.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: cap word-card max height + inner scroll if future content blocks become long again.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb UI: remove nested border+background rows)
- What changed:
  - Updated duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx expansion item row styles from bordered pill blocks to flat list rows.
  - Removed per-item border+background+radius treatment; switched to simple text row with bottom divider and subtle chevron.
  - Added last-row style to drop trailing divider for cleaner list ending.
- What was learned:
  - Flat list rows reduce visual nesting and better match the single-container expansion design direction.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add lightweight press-state opacity only (without introducing container chrome).

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb pager fix: duplicated empty message)
- What changed:
  - Added a stable fallback page height in duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx for expansion pager pages.
  - Unified paging calculations (momentum index + scrollTo anchor + page style) to use effectiveExpansionPageHeight.
  - This prevents multi-page stacking when measured pager height is unavailable/late, eliminating repeated empty-state lines.
- What was learned:
  - Pager UIs must have deterministic page height at first paint; otherwise grouped pages can visually merge.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Optional: add a one-time runtime check for unusually small measured pager height and log for QA.

  - Fixed malformed JSX text closings introduced by corrupted text fragments (restored proper `</Text>` tags).
  - Removed UTF-8 BOM from app/knowledge-absorb.tsx to satisfy lint unicode-bom rule.
- What was learned:
  - Encoding-safe edits must avoid shell replacements that inject escaped literal sequences (`\\n`) into source.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb group integrity fix: source facets only)
- What changed:
  - Removed heuristic keyword-recall fallback from duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts::resolveExpansionNodeRefs.
  - Grouped expansion content now resolves only from entryExpansionMap direct facet links, preserving category integrity.
  - Simplified duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx non-sentence expansion area to render only the active group instead of stacking pager pages.
  - Updated duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.test.ts to assert source-driven grouping rather than inferred POS-based grouping.
- What was learned:
  - Runtime recall is acceptable for recommendation surfaces, but not for semantically named categories such as synonyms, antonyms, collocations, and spoken expressions.

## 2026-04-09 (Knowledge absorb anti-regression: category isolation guard)
- What changed:
  - Added a dedicated regression test in duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.test.ts that creates heavily overlapping labels across synonyms, antonyms, phrases, collocations, patterns, spoken expressions, slang, and idioms.
  - The test asserts exact per-group label sets so any future cross-group leakage fails immediately.
- What was learned:
  - For this surface, category integrity is a contract. If a group is semantically named, it must never be filled by recommendation heuristics.
- Verification:
  - npm run lint -- src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.test.ts src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts app/knowledge-absorb.tsx -> pass.

## 2026-04-10 (Knowledge absorb next-step duplicate root fix)

  - Updated duoxx/src/modules/knowledge-absorb/knowledgeAbsorbEngine.ts so session picking no longer falls back to already-seen roots while unseen roots still remain.

## 2026-04-10 (Pipeline: lexicon graph explorer in main content area)
- What changed:
  - Added backend graph browse APIs in `duoxx_server_link/src/routes/pipeline.js`:
    - `GET /api/pipeline/lexicon/nodes`
    - `GET /api/pipeline/lexicon/nodes/:nodeId/relations`
  - Added service support in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/lexiconGraphService.js` for:
    - scope switch (`active` / `published`)
    - fuzzy search over display text, lemma, definition, POS, headword, aliases
    - paginated node listing and paginated relation listing with group counts
  - Extended frontend API client surface in `duoxx/src/services/lexiconApi.ts`:
    - `listGraphNodes`
    - `listNodeRelations`
    - admin payload/pagination types
  - Added new admin UI panel `duoxx/components/admin/LexiconGraphExplorerPanel.tsx`.
  - Integrated panel into pipeline main area via view toggle in `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx` (`课程内容 | 知识图谱`), and kept explanation side panel hidden in graph view.
  - Extended route test mock coverage in `duoxx_server_link/src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js` for new endpoints.
- What was learned:
  - Existing `KnowledgeNode` workbench and lexical graph are separate systems; to match learning-side graph data, pipeline must read from `LexiconNode/LexiconEdge` and snapshot graph, not the older `KnowledgeNode` model.
  - For admin fuzzy search + pagination with current API client behavior, returning a rich payload object inside `data` is the safest contract.
- Verification:
  - `node --check src/services/lexiconGraphService.js` -> pass.
  - `node --check src/routes/pipeline.js` -> pass.
  - `node --check src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js` -> pass.
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (in `duoxx/`) -> pass.
  - Backend Jest could not be executed in this environment because `cross-env`/`jest` binaries are not available under `duoxx_server_link/node_modules`.
## 2026-04-10 (Pipeline graph `? / ??` placeholder cleanup)
- What changed:
  - Added definition sanitization in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/lexiconGraphService.js`:
    - New helper `sanitizeDefinitionValue` removes placeholder-only values like `?`, `??`, `？？` (and punctuation-only noise) to empty string.
    - New helper `sanitizeNodeView` applies the sanitized definition when returning node payloads.
  - Applied cleanup on both write-path and read-path:
    - write-path: during lexicon batch import node upsert merge.
    - read-path: `listNodes`, `listNodeRelations`, `getNode`, `expandNode`.
  - Result: pipeline graph list/detail no longer shows noisy placeholder definitions as `??`; UI now falls back to `-` for empty definitions.
- What was learned:
  - Even when source assets are imperfect, service-level normalization for obvious placeholder tokens prevents operator UI noise without changing node identity or relation structure.
  - Current local environment cannot reliably connect to Mongo (`ECONNRESET` to localhost:27017), so online data quantification is not available in this session.
- Verification:
  - `node --check src/services/lexiconGraphService.js` -> pass.
  - `node --check src/routes/pipeline.js` -> pass.
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (in `duoxx/`) -> pass.

## 2026-04-14 (Knowledge absorb breadcrumb back button removal + syntax recovery)
- What changed:
  - Repaired `duoxx/app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` after a JSX/string corruption incident that broke TypeScript parsing.
  - Removed the “返回上一层” button from breadcrumb area; users now navigate only by tapping breadcrumb nodes.
  - Kept breadcrumb visibility rule as `navigationStack.length >= 2`, so a single-node path is hidden and multi-level paths remain clickable.
  - Restored learned-progress wiring in this screen (`knowledgeAbsorbProgress` keys, learned count in header, exhausted-state next button).
  - Added back missing `quickActionDisabled` style and rewrote file without BOM.
- What was learned:
  - Large scripted line removals in JSX are high risk; restoring from a clean snapshot and then reapplying explicit deltas is safer than patching broken fragments.
  - Encoding-safe edits must stay in patch-based workflow to avoid accidental mojibake or unterminated string damage.
- Verification:
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (in `duoxx/`) -> pass.
  - `npm run lint -- app/knowledge-absorb.tsx` (in `duoxx/`) -> pass.

## 2026-04-14 (Commit pollution guardrails enabled in duoxx)
- What changed:
  - Added `duoxx/scripts/guard-staged-files.js` to block staged temp files, UTF-8 BOM, mojibake markers, and replacement char `U+FFFD`.
  - Added versioned git hook at `duoxx/.githooks/pre-commit` to enforce the staged-file guard on every commit.
  - Updated `duoxx/package.json` scripts:
    - `guard:staged`
    - `hooks:install`
  - Updated `duoxx/.gitignore` with temp/debug artifact patterns.
  - Added usage doc `duoxx/docs/COMMIT_GUARD.md`.
  - Installed local hook path with `git config core.hooksPath .githooks` in `duoxx`.
- What was learned:
  - Guard scripts can self-trigger when detection markers are embedded literally in the guard source; allowlisting the guard file for marker-literal check avoids deadlock while preserving BOM/U+FFFD checks.
  - The fastest way to reduce encoding regressions is commit-time gatekeeping, not post-merge cleanup.
- Verification:
  - `npm run guard:staged` (duoxx) -> pass on staged guard files.
  - Negative test: staged `tmp-guard-test.txt` was blocked as expected.
  - `git config --get core.hooksPath` (duoxx) -> `.githooks`.

## 2026-04-14 (Commit pollution guardrails enabled in root repo)
- What changed:
  - Added root staged guard script: `scripts/guard-staged-files.js`.
  - Added root pre-commit hook: `.githooks/pre-commit`.
  - Added root ignore patterns in `.gitignore` for temp/debug artifacts.
  - Added root usage doc: `COMMIT_GUARD.md`.
  - Configured root git hook path to `.githooks`.
- What was learned:
  - Root-level protection is needed in addition to submodule protection, otherwise markdown/memory/doc edits at monorepo root can still bypass guardrails.
  - Negative test must use `git add -f` for ignored temp files, otherwise the guard cannot validate the blocked-file path.
- Verification:
  - `node scripts/guard-staged-files.js` (root) -> pass with no staged files.
  - Negative test: force-staged `tmp-root-guard-test.txt` was blocked as expected.
  - `git config --local --get core.hooksPath` (root) -> `.githooks`.

## 2026-04-15 (Operator Review Hub tabs visually clarified)

  - Introduced a segmented tab rail style for `Import / Knowledge Review / Task Review`.
  - Added explicit active affordance (contrast + indicator) and tab accessibility semantics.
- What was learned:
  - Operators identify mode switches faster when tabs share one container and one selected marker, compared with isolated outlined chips.

## 2026-04-16 (Pipeline 极简 3 步流 + 一键发布落地)
- What changed:
  - Frontend `duoxx/components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx`:
    - Replaced dual actions (`导入图谱批次` + `发布快照`) with a single primary action `发布到学习库`.
    - Kept review blocking UI but changed user-facing language to business terms (no batch/snapshot terminology).
    - Added release blocking messages:
      - `未完成审查，暂不可发布。`
      - `质量门禁未通过，暂不可发布。`
    - Continued using candidate review flow (approve/reject/merge) before publish.
  - Frontend API/storage:
    - Added `releaseToLearning` in `duoxx/src/services/lexiconApi.ts`.
    - Added local fallback orchestration `releaseToLearning` in `duoxx/src/storage/lexiconGraphStorage.ts`.
    - Local publish now keeps only one current snapshot record.
  - Backend orchestration:
    - Added `POST /api/pipeline/lexicon/release` in `duoxx_server_link/src/routes/pipeline.js`.
    - Added `releaseToLearning` in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/lexiconGraphService.js`:
      - internal flow: import (if needed) -> pending review gate -> strict quality gate publish.
      - returns `status / blockedReason / pendingReviewCount / publishedAt / currentPublishId`.
    - Updated publish behavior to stage new snapshot, switch active pointer, and clean old snapshots (current-only retention).
  - Tests:
    - Added release endpoint smoke coverage in `duoxx_server_link/src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js`.
    - Added service integration coverage for blocked/published release path and single-current snapshot retention in `duoxx_server_link/src/services/__tests__/lexiconGraphService.integration.test.js`.
- What was learned:
  - Exposing only one publish action reduces operator branching without weakening strict quality gates.
  - Keeping old endpoints as compatibility while routing UI to a single orchestration endpoint gives a clean migration path.
  - `LexiconSnapshot` cleanup after pointer switch is necessary to satisfy “only current version” policy, not only `isActive=false`.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Add route-level contract tests for release payload variants (`batchId` only vs `review/bundleReviews`) when server test env is fully available.
  - Evaluate whether old `/lexicon/import-batches` and `/lexicon/publish` should be internally flagged/deprecated in admin docs.
- Verification:
  - `node --check src/routes/pipeline.js` (duoxx_server_link) -> pass.
  - `node --check src/services/lexiconGraphService.js` (duoxx_server_link) -> pass.
  - `node --check src/routes/lexiconGraphFlow.test.js` (duoxx_server_link) -> pass.
  - `node --check src/services/__tests__/lexiconGraphService.integration.test.js` (duoxx_server_link) -> pass.
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (duoxx) -> pass.
  - Note: Jest execution in `duoxx_server_link` is currently blocked in this environment because `cross-env/jest` binaries are unavailable from local `node_modules`.

## 2026-04-16 (Operator Review Hub 删除 Task Review 并重构为 Import-only)
- What changed:
  - Removed `Task Review` feature from `duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx` at code level:
    - removed tab entry and entire task review UI panel;
    - removed task/candidate review state, data fetching, and action handlers;
    - removed related selector/tab style and helper UI.
  - Reworked page layout to import-first:
    - removed top tab rail;
    - header now uses a compact `Import Workspace` title + metrics + refresh action;
    - body renders import panel directly as single dominant workflow.
  - `reload` now only triggers upstream import-publish refresh callback instead of loading removed task/knowledge queues.
- What was learned:
  - After removing non-core review lanes, keeping a single entry workflow significantly reduces operator context switching.
  - Import-only layout benefits from deleting stale state/fetch code, not just hiding panels.
- Verification:
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (duoxx) -> pass.
  - `npm run lint -- components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx` (duoxx) -> pass.

## 2026-04-16 (Pipeline refresh loop + 429 popup storm fix)
- What changed:
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx`:
    - Refactored `loadCourses` to `useCallback` and added in-flight dedupe (`courseLoadInFlightRef`) to prevent concurrent duplicate requests.
    - Added rate-limit error detection (`isTooManyRequestsApiError`) and 5s throttle for alert display to avoid repeated modal storms.
    - Replaced inline `onImportPublished={() => { void loadCourses(); }}` with stable callback `handleOperatorImportPublished` to stop child effect loops.
  - Updated `duoxx/components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx`:
    - `onImportPublished` prop now supports async callback (`() => void | Promise<void>`).
    - Awaited publish callback after successful publish to keep refresh timing deterministic.
- What was learned:
  - Passing unstable inline callbacks into child `useEffect` dependency chains can create render-triggered request loops and quickly hit backend 429 limits.
  - Request dedupe plus rate-limit alert throttling is needed in admin pages that expose manual refresh actions.
- Next steps / open questions:
  - Consider replacing blocking web `alert` with non-blocking toast for all admin error notifications to avoid modal interruption under transient backend pressure.
- Verification:
  - `npx tsc --noEmit` (duoxx) -> pass.
  - `npm run lint -- components/admin/PipelineDashboard.tsx components/admin/OperatorWorkbench.tsx components/admin/LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx` (duoxx) -> pass (1 existing warning in `LexicalAssetImportPanel.tsx`).

- What was learned:
  - Because `duoxx` is tracked as a gitlink, frontend changes must be committed inside `duoxx` first and then recorded by the root repo.
  - Bulk markdown knowledge updates benefit from a `git diff --check` pass before commit to catch whitespace hygiene issues early.
